    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nimport json\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin\n\n# 1. Ensure workspace exists\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\nprint(f"[INFO] Using workspace: {workspace}\\n")\n\n# 2. Define the exact paper title\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon’s Diet?"\nprint(f"[INFO] Target title: \'{title}\'\\n")\n\n# 3. Query Crossref for the title\ncr_url = \'https://api.crossref.org/works\'\nparams = {\'query.title\': title, \'rows\': 10}\nprint(f"[INFO] Querying Crossref API for works matching title...")\ntry:\n    cr_resp = requests.get(cr_url, params=params, timeout=30)\n    cr_resp.raise_for_status()\n    items = cr_resp.json().get(\'message\', {}).get(\'items\', [])\n    print(f"[INFO] Crossref returned {len(items)} items\\n")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to query Crossref: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nif not items:\n    print("ERROR: No items found in Crossref for the given title.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 4. Inspect returned items and find the best match\nselected = None\nprint("[INFO] Inspecting Crossref candidates:")\nfor idx, item in enumerate(items, start=1):\n    cand_title = item.get(\'title\', [\'\'])[0]\n    doi = item.get(\'DOI\')\n    print(f"  {idx}. Title: {cand_title}\\n     DOI: {doi}\\n")\n    # Exact case-insensitive match\n    if cand_title.strip().lower() == title.strip().lower():\n        selected = item\n        print(f"[INFO] Exact title match found at index {idx}\\n")\n        break\n\n# 5. Fallback to first item if no exact match\nif not selected:\n    selected = items[0]\n    print(f"[WARN] No exact title match; defaulting to first Crossref item:\\n     {selected.get(\'title\', [\'\'])[0]} (DOI: {selected.get(\'DOI\')})\\n")\n\ndoi = selected.get(\'DOI\')\nif not doi:\n    print("ERROR: Selected Crossref item has no DOI; cannot proceed.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"[INFO] Selected DOI: {doi}\\n")\n\n# 6. Look for PDF link in Crossref \'link\' field\npdf_link = None\nlinks = selected.get(\'link\', [])\nprint(f"[INFO] Inspecting Crossref \'link\' entries ({len(links)} total):")\nfor linkobj in links:\n    url = linkobj.get(\'URL\')\n    content_type = linkobj.get(\'content-type\', \'\')\n    print(f"  - URL: {url} (type: {content_type})")\n    if \'application/pdf\' in content_type.lower():\n        pdf_link = url\n        print(f"[INFO] Found PDF via Crossref \'link\' field: {pdf_link}\\n")\n        break\n\n# 7. If no PDF link from Crossref, try Unpaywall\nif not pdf_link:\n    email = os.getenv(\'UNPAY_EMAIL\')\n    if not email:\n        print("[ERROR] No PDF link in Crossref metadata and UNPAY_EMAIL not set.")\n        print("Set the UNPAY_EMAIL environment variable to your email for Unpaywall API access.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    up_url = f\'https://api.unpaywall.org/v2/{doi}\'\n    print(f"[INFO] Querying Unpaywall for DOI {doi}...")\n    try:\n        up_resp = requests.get(up_url, params={\'email\': email}, timeout=30)\n        up_resp.raise_for_status()\n        up_data = up_resp.json()\n        best = up_data.get(\'best_oa_location\', {})\n        pdf_link = best.get(\'url_for_pdf\')\n        if pdf_link:\n            print(f"[INFO] Found PDF via Unpaywall: {pdf_link}\\n")\n        else:\n            print("[ERROR] Unpaywall did not return a PDF URL.")\n            sys.exit(1)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"ERROR: Failed to query Unpaywall: {e}")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n# 8. Final check of pdf_link\nif not pdf_link:\n    print("ERROR: Could not determine any PDF URL for the selected DOI.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 9. Download the PDF\npdf_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nprint(f"[DOWNLOAD] Fetching PDF: {pdf_link}\\n        Saving to: {pdf_path}\\n")\nheaders = {\'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\', \'Accept\': \'application/pdf\'}\ntotal = 0\ntry:\n    with requests.get(pdf_link, headers=headers, stream=True, timeout=60) as r:\n        r.raise_for_status()\n        with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n            for chunk in r.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n                if chunk:\n                    f.write(chunk)\n                    total += len(chunk)\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 10. Report results\nprint(f"[DONE] Download complete: {total} bytes ({total/1024/1024:.2f} MB)")\nif total < 10_000:\n    print("[WARN] File size <10 KB; may be incomplete.")\nelse:\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] PDF saved at {pdf_path}")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# Step 1: Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.exists(workspace):\n    print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{workspace}\' does not exist.")\n    print("Please run the search scripts first to generate HTML files.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"[INFO] Using workspace: {workspace}\\n")\n\n# Step 2: Define paths to saved search HTML files\nddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_duckduckgo_search.html\')\nbing_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_bing_search.html\')\n\n# Step 3: Verify HTML files exist\nfor path in (ddg_html, bing_html):\n    if not os.path.exists(path):\n        print(f"ERROR: Missing required file: {path}")\n        print("Run the site-specific search step first to save HTML files.")\n        sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"[INFO] Found HTML files:\\n - {ddg_html}\\n - {bing_html}\\n")\n\n# Container for detected Leicester links\nleicester_links = []\n\n# Helper to extract and print Leicester-related URLs\ndef inspect_file(file_path, label):\n    print(f"[INSPECT] Searching for \'le.ac.uk\' links in {label}...\\n")\n    with open(file_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        content = f.read()\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(content, \'html.parser\')\n    # Check all <a> hrefs\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        # Direct Leicester links\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in href:\n            print(f"  [DIRECT] {label} --> {href}")\n            leicester_links.append(href)\n        # DuckDuckGo uddg redirect links\n        if \'/l/?uddg=\' in href:\n            parsed = urlparse(href)\n            q = parse_qs(parsed.query).get(\'uddg\', [])\n            if q:\n                real = unquote(q[0])\n                if \'le.ac.uk\' in real:\n                    print(f"  [REDIRECT] {label} uddg decoded --> {real}")\n                    leicester_links.append(real)\n    # Fallback: raw text search for any \'le.ac.uk\' occurrences\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in line and \'<a \' not in line:\n            # Print context window\n            start = max(0, i-2)\n            end = min(len(lines), i+3)\n            print(f"  [TEXT] Context around line {i+1}:")\n            for j in range(start, end):\n                print(f"    {j+1}: {lines[j].strip()}")\n            print()\n\n# Inspect DuckDuckGo HTML\ntry:\n    inspect_file(ddg_html, \'DuckDuckGo HTML\')\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR while inspecting DuckDuckGo file: {e}")\n\nprint("\\n" + "-"*60 + "\\n")\n\n# Inspect Bing HTML\ntry:\n    inspect_file(bing_html, \'Bing HTML\')\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR while inspecting Bing file: {e}")\n\n# Deduplicate Leicester links\nunique_leicester = []\nfor url in leicester_links:\n    if url not in unique_leicester:\n        unique_leicester.append(url)\n\n# Save inspection results to a local text file\noutput_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\')\nwith open(output_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as out_f:\n    out_f.write(\'Detected Leicester domain links and contexts:\\n\\n\')\n    for url in unique_leicester:\n        out_f.write(f"{url}\\n")\n\nprint(f"[DONE] Inspection complete. Found {len(unique_leicester)} unique Leicester links.")\nprint(f"[INFO] Detailed report saved to: {output_path}")\nprint("Next: Review \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\' to identify the correct PDF URL pattern on \'le.ac.uk\'.")',

    "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote, urljoin\n\n# 1. Ensure workspace exists\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\nprint(f"[INFO] Using workspace: {workspace}\\n")\n\n# 2. Allow override via environment variable\noverride_pdf = os.getenv(\'DRAGON_PDF_URL\')\nif override_pdf:\n    print(f"[INFO] DRAGON_PDF_URL override detected: {override_pdf}\\n")\n    landing_pdf = override_pdf\nelse:\n    # 3. Define saved search HTML files\n    ddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_duckduckgo_search.html\')\n    bing_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_bing_search.html\')\n    for path in (ddg_html, bing_html):\n        if not os.path.exists(path):\n            print(f"ERROR: Missing required file: {path}")\n            sys.exit(1)\n    print(f"[INFO] Found search HTML:\\n - {ddg_html}\\n - {bing_html}\\n")\n\n    # 4. Extract landing page URLs on le.ac.uk\n    def parse_search_for_leicester(html_path, label):\n        urls = []\n        print(f"[PARSE] Looking for Leicester landing links in {label}...")\n        with open(html_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(f, \'html.parser\')\n        for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n            href = a[\'href\']\n            # handle DuckDuckGo uddg redirects\n            if \'/l/?uddg=\' in href:\n                parsed = urlparse(href)\n                q = parse_qs(parsed.query).get(\'uddg\', [])\n                if q:\n                    href = unquote(q[0])\n            # absolute or relative\n            full = href\n            # ensure we have absolute URL\n            if not urlparse(full).scheme:\n                continue\n            if \'le.ac.uk\' in urlparse(full).netloc.lower():\n                print(f"  [FOUND] {full}")\n                urls.append(full)\n        return urls\n\n    ddg_links = parse_search_for_leicester(ddg_html, \'DuckDuckGo\')\n    bing_links = parse_search_for_leicester(bing_html, \'Bing\')\n    landing_links = []\n    for u in ddg_links + bing_links:\n        if u not in landing_links:\n            landing_links.append(u)\n    print(f"\\n[INFO] Unique Leicester landing URLs: {len(landing_links)}\\n")\n\n    if not landing_links:\n        print("ERROR: No le.ac.uk landing pages found.\\n       Please inspect the HTML files or set DRAGON_PDF_URL to the direct PDF URL.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 5. For each landing page, fetch and search for .pdf link\n    landing_pdf = None\n    for idx, page_url in enumerate(landing_links, start=1):\n        print(f"[FETCH] Landing page {idx}/{len(landing_links)}: {page_url}")\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(page_url, headers={\'User-Agent\':\'Mozilla/5.0\'}, timeout=20)\n            resp.raise_for_status()\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"  [WARN] Could not fetch landing page: {e}\\n")\n            continue\n        soup2 = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n        pdf_candidates = []\n        for a in soup2.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n            href2 = a[\'href\']\n            if href2.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in href2.lower():\n                full_pdf = urljoin(page_url, href2)\n                pdf_candidates.append(full_pdf)\n        if pdf_candidates:\n            landing_pdf = pdf_candidates[0]\n            print(f"  [FOUND] PDF link on page: {landing_pdf}\\n")\n            break\n        else:\n            print("  [INFO] No PDF links on this landing page.\\n")\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    if not landing_pdf:\n        print("ERROR: No PDF link found on any landing pages.\\n       Please set DRAGON_PDF_URL or refine the parser.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n# 6. Download the identified PDF\npdf_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nprint(f"[DOWNLOAD] Downloading PDF from: {landing_pdf}\\n         to: {pdf_path}\\n")\nsize = 0\ntry:\n    with requests.get(landing_pdf, headers={\'User-Agent\':\'Mozilla/5.0\',\'Accept\':\'application/pdf\'}, stream=True, timeout=60) as r:\n        r.raise_for_status()\n        with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n            for chunk in r.iter_content(8192):\n                if chunk:\n                    f.write(chunk)\n                    size += len(chunk)\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 7. Final report\nprint(f"[DONE] Download complete: {size} bytes ({size/1024/1024:.2f} MB)")\nif size < 10_000:\n    print("WARNING: File size <10 KB; may be incomplete or incorrect.")\nelse:\n    print(f"SUCCESS: PDF saved at {pdf_path}")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote\n\n# Step 1: Ensure workspace exists and contains the search result HTML files\ndir_workspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(dir_workspace):\n    print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{dir_workspace}\' does not exist.")\n    print("Please run the search scripts first to save the DuckDuckGo and Bing HTML files.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nfile_ddg = os.path.join(dir_workspace, \'site_le_duckduckgo_search.html\')\nfile_bing = os.path.join(dir_workspace, \'site_le_bing_search.html\')\nfor fpath in (file_ddg, file_bing):\n    if not os.path.isfile(fpath):\n        print(f"ERROR: Required file not found: {fpath}")\n        print("Make sure you have saved the search result pages into workspace/ before running this.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Inspecting for \'le.ac.uk\' links in:\\n - {file_ddg}\\n - {file_bing}\\n")\n\n# Container for all detected le.ac.uk URLs\nleicester_urls = []\n\ndef inspect_html(path, label):\n    """\n    Parse the given HTML file for any links to le.ac.uk, including\n    direct <a href> and DuckDuckGo uddg redirect links, plus raw text occurrences.\n    """\n    print(f"[INSPECT] {label}")\n    with open(path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        raw = f.read()\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(raw, \'html.parser\')\n\n    # 1) Check all <a> tags\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        # handle DuckDuckGo redirect pattern (/l/?uddg=...)\n        if \'/l/?uddg=\' in href:\n            parsed = urlparse(href)\n            q = parse_qs(parsed.query).get(\'uddg\', [])\n            if q:\n                decoded = unquote(q[0])\n                if \'le.ac.uk\' in urlparse(decoded).netloc.lower():\n                    print(f"  [REDIRECT] decoded uddg -> {decoded}")\n                    leicester_urls.append(decoded)\n        # direct link\n        net = urlparse(href).netloc.lower()\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in net:\n            print(f"  [DIRECT] {href}")\n            leicester_urls.append(href)\n\n    # 2) Raw text scan for any \'le.ac.uk\' not in an <a> tag\n    lines = raw.splitlines()\n    for idx, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in line and \'<a \' not in line:\n            start = max(0, idx - 2)\n            end = min(len(lines), idx + 3)\n            print(f"  [TEXT] Context around line {idx+1}:")\n            for i in range(start, end):\n                print(f"    {i+1:4d}: {lines[i].strip()}")\n            print(\'\')\n\n# Run inspection on both files\ninspect_html(file_ddg, \'DuckDuckGo results\')\nprint(\'-\' * 60)\ninspect_html(file_bing, \'Bing results\')\n\n# Deduplicate\nunique = []\nfor u in leicester_urls:\n    if u not in unique:\n        unique.append(u)\n\n# Step 4: Write to output report\nout_path = os.path.join(dir_workspace, \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\')\nwith open(out_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as out_f:\n    out_f.write(\'Detected University of Leicester (le.ac.uk) landing URLs and contexts:\\n\\n\')\n    for url in unique:\n        out_f.write(url + \'\\n\')\n\nprint(f"[DONE] Found {len(unique)} unique Leicester-related URLs.")\nprint(f"[INFO] Detailed list written to: {out_path}")\nprint("Next: Open and review \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\' to identify the correct landing-page URL(s) on le.ac.uk for the target paper.")',

{
    "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote\n\n# Step 1: Define workspace and verify its existence\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{workspace}\' does not exist.")\n    print("Please ensure that search result HTML files are saved in the workspace directory.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Step 2: Define the expected search-result HTML file paths\nddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_duckduckgo_search.html\')\nbing_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'site_le_bing_search.html\')\nfor html_file in (ddg_html, bing_html):\n    if not os.path.isfile(html_file):\n        print(f"ERROR: Required file not found: {html_file}")\n        print("Make sure you\'ve saved the DuckDuckGo and Bing search-result HTML into workspace/ before running this tool.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Inspecting for \'le.ac.uk\' links in:\\n - {ddg_html}\\n - {bing_html}\\n")\n\n# Container for all detected University of Leicester URLs\nleicester_urls = []\n\n# Function to inspect one HTML file for le.ac.uk URLs using regex parsing\ndef inspect_html(path, label):\n    print(f"[INSPECT] {label}")\n    with open(path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\', errors=\'ignore\') as f:\n        raw = f.read()\n\n    # 1) Regex to find all href attributes\n    href_pattern = re.compile(r\'<a\\s+[^>]*href=["\\\']([^"\\\']+)["\\\']\', re.IGNORECASE)\n    for match in href_pattern.finditer(raw):\n        href = match.group(1)\n        # Handle DuckDuckGo redirect (/l/?uddg=...)\n        if \'/l/?uddg=\' in href:\n            parsed = urlparse(href)\n            q = parse_qs(parsed.query).get(\'uddg\', [])\n            if q:\n                decoded = unquote(q[0])\n                host = urlparse(decoded).netloc.lower()\n                if \'le.ac.uk\' in host:\n                    print(f"  [REDIRECT] decoded uddg -> {decoded}")\n                    leicester_urls.append(decoded)\n        # Direct link with le.ac.uk in netloc\n        try:\n            netloc = urlparse(href).netloc.lower()\n        except Exception:\n            netloc = \'\'\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in netloc:\n            print(f"  [DIRECT] {href}")\n            leicester_urls.append(href)\n\n    # 2) Raw text scan for le.ac.uk occurrences outside <a> tags\n    lines = raw.splitlines()\n    for idx, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if \'le.ac.uk\' in line and \'<a \' not in line.lower():\n            start = max(0, idx - 2)\n            end = min(len(lines), idx + 3)\n            print(f"  [TEXT] Context around line {idx+1}:")\n            for i in range(start, end):\n                print(f"    {i+1:4d}: {lines[i].strip()}")\n            print("")\n\n# Inspect both search-result pages\ninspect_html(ddg_html, \'DuckDuckGo results\')\nprint(\'-\' * 60)\ninspect_html(bing_html, \'Bing results\')\n\n# Deduplicate found URLs\nunique_urls = []\nfor url in leicester_urls:\n    if url not in unique_urls:\n        unique_urls.append(url)\n\n# Step 4: Write the inspection report\nreport_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\')\nwith open(report_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as out_f:\n    out_f.write(\'Detected University of Leicester (le.ac.uk) landing URLs and contexts:\\n\\n\')\n    for url in unique_urls:\n        out_f.write(url + \'\\n\')\n\nprint(f"[DONE] Found {len(unique_urls)} unique Leicester-related URLs.")\nprint(f"[INFO] Detailed list written to: {report_path}")\nprint("Next: Open and review \'leicester_link_inspection.txt\' to identify the correct landing-page URL(s) on le.ac.uk for the target paper.")',

match http(s) URLs ending in .pdf, stopping at space, \' or \\" or >\nall_pdfs = re.findall(pattern, html)\nprint(f"[PARSE] Found {len(all_pdfs)} total .pdf URLs in the HTML.")\n\n# Step 4: Filter for le.ac.uk domain\nleicester_pdfs = [link for link in set(all_pdfs) if \'le.ac.uk\' in link.lower()]\nprint(f"[FILTER] {len(leicester_pdfs)} PDF links on le.ac.uk domain found.")\nfor link in leicester_pdfs:\n    print(f"  [MATCH] {link}")\n\nif not leicester_pdfs:\n    print("ERROR: No .pdf links on le.ac.uk found in Bing results.")\n    print("Please verify that the paper is hosted on le.ac.uk or adjust the query.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Step 5: Download the first matching PDF\npdf_url = leicester_pdfs[0]\npdf_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nprint(f"[DOWNLOAD] Downloading PDF from: {pdf_url}")\ntry:\n    rpdf = requests.get(pdf_url, headers=headers, stream=True, timeout=60)\n    rpdf.raise_for_status()\n    with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n        for chunk in rpdf.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n            if chunk:\n                f.write(chunk)\n    size = os.path.getsize(pdf_path)\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF to: {pdf_path}")\n    print(f"[INFO] File size: {size} bytes ({size/1024:.2f} KB)")\n    if size < 10 * 1024:\n        print("WARNING: PDF file is smaller than 10 KB. It may not be the correct paper.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    print("[COMPLETE] PDF download appears successful and exceeds size threshold.")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n    if os.path.exists(pdf_path):\n        os.remove(pdf_path)\n    sys.exit(1)',
    "description": 'We fixed the regex quoting issue that previously caused a SyntaxError by using a double-quoted Python raw string (`pattern = r"https?://[^\\\\s\\\\\\"\'>]+\\\\.pdf"`) which properly escapes both quotes and stops at whitespace, quotes or `>` characters.     "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin\n\n# Step 1: Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{workspace}\' does not exist.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"[INFO] Using workspace: {workspace}\\n")\n\n# Common headers for requests\nHEADERS = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \'\n                  \'AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \'\n                  \'Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html\'\n}\n\n# Utility to perform a Bing search and return HTML\ndef bing_search(query):\n    url = \'https://www.bing.com/search\'\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Bing query: {query}")\n    resp = requests.get(url, params={\'q\': query}, headers=HEADERS, timeout=30)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Retrieved {len(resp.text)} characters of HTML")\n    return resp.text\n\n# Phase 1: Look for landing page on le.ac.uk containing the paper title\ntitle_phrase = \'Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon’s Diet?\'\nphase1_query = f"site:le.ac.uk \\"{title_phrase}\\""\nhtml1 = bing_search(phase1_query)\n\n# Extract all href URLs from search results\nhrefs1 = re.findall(r\'href=["\'](https?://[^"\'> ]+)["\']\', html1)\nle_urls = [u for u in hrefs1 if \'le.ac.uk\' in u.lower()]\nle_urls = list(dict.fromkeys(le_urls))  # dedupe preserving order\nprint(f"[PARSE] Found {len(le_urls)} candidate landing URLs on le.ac.uk:")\nfor i, u in enumerate(le_urls[:5], 1):\n    print(f"  {i}. {u}")\n\npdf_url = None\n# If we have a landing URL, fetch it and look for .pdf links\nif le_urls:\n    landing = le_urls[0]\n    print(f"\\n[PHASE1] Fetching landing page: {landing}")\n    try:\n        lp_resp = requests.get(landing, headers=HEADERS, timeout=30)\n        lp_resp.raise_for_status()\n        lp_html = lp_resp.text\n        # Find PDF links on landing page (absolute or relative)\n        pdfs_lp = re.findall(r\'href=["\']([^"\'>]+\\.pdf(?:\\?[^"\'>]*)?)["\']\', lp_html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n        pdfs_lp = list(dict.fromkeys(pdfs_lp))\n        print(f"[PHASE1] Found {len(pdfs_lp)} .pdf links on landing page.")\n        for p in pdfs_lp[:5]:\n            full = urljoin(landing, p)\n            print(f"   -> {full}")\n        if pdfs_lp:\n            pdf_url = urljoin(landing, pdfs_lp[0])\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"ERROR: Failed to fetch/parse landing page: {e}")\n\n# Phase 2: Fallback search directly for PDF if Phase 1 failed\nif not pdf_url:\n    print("\\n[PHASE2] No PDF found on landing page. Falling back to broad PDF search.")\n    phase2_query = f"\\"{title_phrase}\\" filetype:pdf"\n    html2 = bing_search(phase2_query)\n    # Extract all PDF URLs (with optional query strings)\n    pattern = r"https?://[^\\s\'\\">]+\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s\'\\">]*)?"\n    all_pdfs = re.findall(pattern, html2, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    all_pdfs = list(dict.fromkeys(all_pdfs))\n    print(f"[PARSE] Extracted {len(all_pdfs)} total PDF URLs from HTML.")\n    for i, p in enumerate(all_pdfs[:10], 1):\n        print(f"  {i}. {p}")\n    if not all_pdfs:\n        print("ERROR: No PDF URLs found in fallback search. Cannot proceed.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    # Prefer PDFs on le.ac.uk but allow any\n    le_pdfs = [p for p in all_pdfs if \'le.ac.uk\' in p.lower()]\n    if le_pdfs:\n        print(f"[FILTER] {len(le_pdfs)} PDF URLs on le.ac.uk domain found in fallback.")\n        pdf_url = le_pdfs[0]\n    else:\n        print("[FILTER] No le.ac.uk PDFs in fallback. Picking first available PDF URL.")\n        pdf_url = all_pdfs[0]\n    print(f"[SELECT] PDF URL chosen: {pdf_url}")\n\n# Step: Download the chosen PDF\npdf_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nprint(f"\\n[DOWNLOAD] Downloading PDF to: {pdf_path}")\ntry:\n    r = requests.get(pdf_url, headers=HEADERS, stream=True, timeout=60)\n    r.raise_for_status()\n    with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n        for chunk in r.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n            if chunk:\n                f.write(chunk)\n    size = os.path.getsize(pdf_path)\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF ({size} bytes, {size/1024:.2f} KB)")\n    if size < 10 * 1024:\n        print("WARNING: File smaller than 10 KB. It may not be the correct PDF.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    print("[COMPLETE] PDF download successful and exceeds size threshold.")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n    if os.path.exists(pdf_path):\n        os.remove(pdf_path)\n    sys.exit(1)',

We pivot to a two-phase strategy to locate and download the PDF:\n   • Phase 1: Search for a landing page on le.ac.uk containing the exact paper title. Win64; x64) \'\n                  \'AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \'\n                  \'Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html\'\n}\nprint(f"[SEARCH] Querying Bing for PDF: {query}")\ntry:\n    resp = requests.get(search_url, params={\'q\': query}, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    html = resp.text\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Retrieved {len(html)} characters of HTML from Bing.")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to fetch Bing search results: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Step 3: Extract all PDF URLs (with optional query strings)\npattern = r"https?://[^\\s\\"\'<>]+\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s\\"\'<>]*)?"\nall_pdfs = re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\nprint(f"[PARSE] Extracted {len(all_pdfs)} total PDF URLs from Bing HTML.")\nif all_pdfs:\n    for i, url in enumerate(all_pdfs[:20], 1):\n        print(f"  {i}. {url}")\nelse:\n    print("[PARSE] No PDF URLs found in Bing results.")\n\n# Step 4: Choose the best candidate\n# Prefer URLs that contain keywords from the title\ncandidates = [u for u in all_pdfs if any(k in u.lower() for k in [\'hiccup\', \'dragon\', \'fish\'])]\nif candidates:\n    print(f"[FILTER] {len(candidates)} candidate(s) matched title keywords.")\n    pdf_url = candidates[0]\nelse:\n    if all_pdfs:\n        print("[FILTER] No keyword match; defaulting to first PDF URL found.")\n        pdf_url = all_pdfs[0]\n    else:\n        print("ERROR: No PDF URLs available to download.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[SELECT] PDF URL chosen: {pdf_url}\\n")\n\n# Step 5: Download the chosen PDF into workspace/dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\npdf_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nprint(f"[DOWNLOAD] Downloading PDF to: {pdf_path}")\ntry:\n    r = requests.get(pdf_url, headers=headers, stream=True, timeout=60)\n    r.raise_for_status()\n    with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as f:\n        for chunk in r.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n            if chunk:\n                f.write(chunk)\n    size = os.path.getsize(pdf_path)\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF ({size} bytes, {size/1024:.2f} KB)")\n    if size < 10 * 1024:\n        print("WARNING: File smaller than 10 KB.     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport requests\n\ndef ensure_workspace():\n    workspace = \'workspace\'\n    if not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n        print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{workspace}\' does not exist.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    return workspace\n\n# Utility: download a PDF from a URL into workspace\ndef download_pdf(pdf_url, dest_path):\n    print(f"[DOWNLOAD] Attempting download from: {pdf_url}")\n    try:\n        r = requests.get(pdf_url, headers=HEADERS, stream=True, timeout=60)\n        r.raise_for_status()\n        with open(dest_path, \'wb\') as f:\n            for chunk in r.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n                if chunk:\n                    f.write(chunk)\n        size = os.path.getsize(dest_path)\n        print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF to: {dest_path} ({size} bytes, {size/1024:.2f} KB)")\n        if size < 10 * 1024:\n            print("WARNING: File smaller than 10 KB. It may not be the correct PDF.")\n            sys.exit(1)\n        print("[COMPLETE] PDF download successful and exceeds size threshold.")\n        return True\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"ERROR: Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n        if os.path.exists(dest_path):\n            os.remove(dest_path)\n        return False\n\n# Search via Bing for filetype:pdf\ndef search_bing(title):\n    print(f"[PHASE] Bing search for: \\"{title}\\" filetype:pdf")\n    resp = requests.get(\n        \'https://www.bing.com/search\',\n        params={\'q\': f\'"{title}" filetype:pdf\'},\n        headers=HEADERS,\n        timeout=30\n    )\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    html = resp.text\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Retrieved {len(html)} chars of HTML from Bing.")\n    return html\n\n# Search via DuckDuckGo HTML for filetype:pdf\ndef search_ddg(title):\n    print(f"[PHASE] DuckDuckGo search for: \\"{title}\\" filetype:pdf")\n    resp = requests.get(\n        \'https://duckduckgo.com/html/\',\n        data={\'q\': f\'"{title}" filetype:pdf\'},\n        headers=HEADERS,\n        timeout=30\n    )\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    html = resp.text\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Retrieved {len(html)} chars of HTML from DuckDuckGo.")\n    return html\n\n# Extract PDF URLs from HTML using robust regex\ndef extract_pdfs(html):\n    pattern = r"https?://[^\\s\\"\'<>()]+\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s\\"\'<>()]*)?"\n    matches = re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\n    unique = list(dict.fromkeys(matches))  # dedupe\n    print(f"[PARSE] Extracted {len(unique)} unique PDF URLs.")\n    for i, url in enumerate(unique[:20], 1):\n        print(f"  {i}. {url}")\n    return unique\n\n# Main logic\nif __name__ == \'__main__\':\n    HEADERS = {\n        \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \'\n                      \'AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \'\n                      \'Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\',\n        \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n        \'Accept\': \'text/html\'\n    }\n\n    workspace = ensure_workspace()\n    title = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n    dest_pdf = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\n    # 1) Check for manual override via environment variable\n    manual_url = os.getenv(\'DRAGON_PDF_URL\')\n    if manual_url:\n        print(f"[OVERRIDE] Using DRAGON_PDF_URL: {manual_url}")\n        if download_pdf(manual_url, dest_pdf):\n            sys.exit(0)\n        else:\n            sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 2) Phase 1: Bing search\n    html_bing = search_bing(title)\n    pdfs = extract_pdfs(html_bing)\n\n    # 3) If none, Phase 2: DuckDuckGo search\n    if not pdfs:\n        html_ddg = search_ddg(title)\n        pdfs = extract_pdfs(html_ddg)\n\n    if not pdfs:\n        print("ERROR: No PDF URLs found from both Bing and DuckDuckGo searches.")\n        print("Please manually locate the PDF URL and set DRAGON_PDF_URL environment variable.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 4) Filter candidates by keywords\n    kws = [\'hiccup\', \'dragon\', \'fish\', \'le.ac.uk\']\n    candidates = [u for u in pdfs if any(k in u.lower() for k in kws)]\n    if candidates:\n        print(f"[FILTER] {len(candidates)} candidate(s) matched keywords {kws}")\n        pdf_url = candidates[0]\n    else:\n        print("[FILTER] No keyword match; defaulting to first extracted PDF URL.")\n        pdf_url = pdfs[0]\n\n    print(f"[SELECT] PDF URL chosen: {pdf_url}\\n")\n\n    # 5) Download\n    success = download_pdf(pdf_url, dest_pdf)\n    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)\n',
    "description": 'Implementation Rationale and Next Steps:\n\n1. **Workspace Check**: Ensures `workspace/` exists before proceeding.\n2. **Manual Override**: If the tester or environment provides `DRAGON_PDF_URL`, the script will immediately download from that URL and exit successfully or fail if the download is invalid.\n3. **Phase 1 (Bing)**: Searches Bing for `"Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?" filetype:pdf`, retrieves HTML, and extracts PDF URLs using a robust regex that handles query parameters and avoids quote/bracket mismatches.\n4. **Phase 2 (DuckDuckGo)**: If the Bing phase yields no URLs, falls back to DuckDuckGo’s HTML search for the same query.\n5. **Extraction and Inspection**: Prints up to the first 20 PDF URLs discovered, so the tester can inspect them for correctness.\n6. **Filtering**: Prefers URLs containing key terms (`hiccup`, `dragon`, `fish`, `le.ac.uk`) to auto-select the most likely match; otherwise uses the first found URL.\n7. **Download and Verification**: Streams the chosen PDF into `workspace/dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf`, verifies size >10 KB, and reports success or failure.\n\nFile Created on Success:\n- workspace/dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf — the downloaded full-text PDF\n\nThis approach addresses previous 0-URL issues by broadening search engines, inspecting all extracted PDF links, and enabling a manual override. After running, the tester should verify the printed list of PDF URLs, confirm the correct URL was chosen, and check that `dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf` exists and exceeds 10 KB.\n',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nWORKSPACE = \'workspace\'\nPDF_DEST = os.path.join(WORKSPACE, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\nTITLE = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\nQUERY = f\'"{TITLE}" filetype:pdf\'\nHEADERS = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) \'\n                  \'AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) \'\n                  \'Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html\'\n}\n\n# --- Helpers ---\ndef ensure_workspace():\n    if not os.path.isdir(WORKSPACE):\n        print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{WORKSPACE}\' not found.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    print(f"[INFO] Workspace: {WORKSPACE}")\n\n\ndef save_html(name, html):\n    path = os.path.join(WORKSPACE, name)\n    with open(path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        f.write(html)\n    print(f"[SAVE] HTML saved to {path}")\n    return path\n\n\ndef extract_pdf_links(html):\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n    urls = set()\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        # normalize relative URLs\n        if href.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in href.lower():\n            urls.add(href)\n    print(f"[PARSE] Found {len(urls)} PDF links via <a> tags.")\n    for i, url in enumerate(urls, 1):\n        print(f"  {i}. {url}")\n    return list(urls)\n\n\ndef download_pdf(url, dest):\n    print(f"[DOWNLOAD] Downloading PDF from: {url}")\n    r = requests.get(url, headers=HEADERS, stream=True, timeout=60)\n    r.raise_for_status()\n    with open(dest, \'wb\') as f:\n        for chunk in r.iter_content(8192):\n            if chunk:\n                f.write(chunk)\n    size = os.path.getsize(dest)\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF ({size} bytes) to {dest}")\n    return size\n\n# --- Main Flow ---\nif __name__ == \'__main__\':\n    ensure_workspace()\n\n    # 1) Bing Search\n    print(f"[SEARCH] Bing for: {QUERY}")\n    bing_resp = requests.get(\'https://www.bing.com/search\', params={\'q\': QUERY}, headers=HEADERS, timeout=30)\n    bing_resp.raise_for_status()\n    html_bing = bing_resp.text\n    save_html(\'bing_search.html\', html_bing)\n    pdf_links = extract_pdf_links(html_bing)\n\n    # 2) DuckDuckGo if needed\n    if not pdf_links:\n        print("[INFO] No PDFs from Bing, falling back to DuckDuckGo...")\n        ddg_resp = requests.post(\'https://duckduckgo.com/html/\', data={\'q\': QUERY}, headers=HEADERS, timeout=30)\n        ddg_resp.raise_for_status()\n        html_ddg = ddg_resp.text\n        save_html(\'ddg_search.html\', html_ddg)\n        pdf_links = extract_pdf_links(html_ddg)\n\n    if not pdf_links:\n        print("ERROR: No PDF URLs found on either search. Cannot proceed.")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 3) Filter candidates by university domain hints\n    keywords = [\'le.ac.uk\', \'lra.le.ac.uk\', \'core.ac.uk\', \'hdl.handle.net\']\n    filtered = [u for u in pdf_links if any(k in u.lower() for k in keywords)]\n    chosen = filtered[0] if filtered else pdf_links[0]\n    print(f"[SELECT] Chosen PDF URL: {chosen}\\n")\n\n    # 4) Download the selected PDF\n    try:\n        size = download_pdf(chosen, PDF_DEST)\n        if size < 10 * 1024:\n            print("WARNING: Downloaded PDF is smaller than 10KB. It may not be correct.")\n            sys.exit(1)\n        print("[COMPLETE] Paper downloaded successfully.")\n        sys.exit(0)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"ERROR: Download failed: {e}")\n        if os.path.exists(PDF_DEST):\n            os.remove(PDF_DEST)\n        sys.exit(1)\n',
    "description": 'This script advances our PLAN by:\n1. Ensuring we have a valid `workspace/` directory.\n2. Defining a robust HTML‐parsing approach using BeautifulSoup to locate `<a href="…pdf">` links instead of brittle regex.\n3. Performing a Bing search for the exact paper title plus `filetype:pdf`, saving the raw HTML (`workspace/bing_search.html`), and extracting PDF links.\n4. Falling back to DuckDuckGo if Bing yields no PDF URLs, saving that HTML (`workspace/ddg_search.html`), and re‐attempting extraction.\n5. Printing all discovered PDF URLs and applying a domain‐hint filter (e.g., `le.ac.uk`, `core.ac.uk`, `hdl.handle.net`) to pick the most likely University of Leicester source.\n6. Downloading the chosen PDF to `workspace/dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf`, verifying its size (>10KB), and reporting success.\n\nFiles created:\n- workspace/bing_search.html — raw Bing search HTML\n- workspace/ddg_search.html — raw DuckDuckGo search HTML (if used)\n- workspace/dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf — final downloaded paper\n\nThis iteration directly addresses the lack of PDF links in the previous HTML by using a proper HTML parser and adding a fallback search engine. Please run the search script first.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nif not os.path.isfile(html_file):\n    print(f"ERROR: HTML file not found at {html_file}. Please generate it with the debug script.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Loading Bing search HTML from: {html_file}\\n")\nwith open(html_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\n\n# Parse HTML\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 1) Extract main search result links (li.b_algo > h2 > a)\nalgo_links = []\nfor li in soup.find_all(\'li\', class_=\'b_algo\'):\n    a = li.find(\'h2\') and li.find(\'h2\').find(\'a\')\n    if a and a.has_attr(\'href\'):\n        title = a.get_text(strip=True)\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        algo_links.append((title, href))\n\n# 2) Extract all anchor links as fallback\nall_links = []\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    text = a.get_text(strip=True)\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    all_links.append((text, href))\n\n# Report counts\nprint(f"[PARSE] Found {len(algo_links)} main result links (li.b_algo > h2 > a)")\nprint(f"[PARSE] Found {len(all_links)} total <a> tags with href\\n")\n\n# Print first 10 main result links for inspection\nprint("[SAMPLE] First 10 main search result links:")\nfor idx, (title, href) in enumerate(algo_links[:10], 1):\n    print(f" {idx}. {title}\\n    -> {href}")\n\n# Print first 10 anchor links containing \'pdf\' substring\npdf_in_anchors = [(t, u) for (t, u) in all_links if \'.pdf\' in u.lower()]\nprint(f"\\n[PARSE] Found {len(pdf_in_anchors)} anchor hrefs containing \'.pdf\'; listing first 10:")\nfor idx, (text, href) in enumerate(pdf_in_anchors[:10], 1):\n    print(f" {idx}. Text: \'{text}\'\\n    -> {href}")\n\n# Save outputs for manual review\nwith open(algo_links_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for title, href in algo_links:\n        f.write(f"{title}\\t{href}\\n")\nprint(f"\\n[SAVE] Main algorithmic links written to: {algo_links_file}")\n\nwith open(all_links_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for text, href in all_links:\n        f.write(f"{text}\\t{href}\\n")\nprint(f"[SAVE] All anchor links written to: {all_links_file}")',

    "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nhtml_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'bing_search.html\')\nout_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'found_pdf_urls.txt\')\n\n# --- Preconditions ---\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    print(f"ERROR: Workspace directory \'{workspace}\' does not exist. Run the search script first.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nif not os.path.isfile(html_path):\n    print(f"ERROR: Bing search HTML not found at {html_path}. Please generate it first.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"[INFO] Reading HTML from: {html_path}\\n")\n\n# --- Load HTML ---\nwith open(html_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\npdf_urls = set()\n\n# 1) Extract direct <a href> links containing ".pdf"\nprint("[STEP] Extracting literal .pdf hrefs from <a> tags...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in href.lower():\n        pdf_urls.add(href)\nprint(f"    Found {len(pdf_urls)} direct .pdf hrefs so far.")\n\n# 2) Handle Bing redirect links (/url? q=...pdf)\nprint("[STEP] Extracting Bing redirect links (/url?q=...pdf)...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.startswith(\'/url?\') or \'bing.com/url?\' in href:\n        parsed = urlparse(href)\n        qs = parse_qs(parsed.query)\n        for key in (\'q\', \'u\', \'url\'):\n            if key in qs:\n                real = qs[key][0]\n                # decode percent-encoding\n                real = unquote(real)\n                if real.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in real.lower():\n                    pdf_urls.add(real)\n                break\nprint(f"    Total after redirect extraction: {len(pdf_urls)} candidates.")\n\n# 3) Regex fallback: full URLs in HTML text\nprint("[STEP] Running regex fallback to catch any PDF URLs in page text...")\npattern = r\'https?://[^\\s"\\\']+?\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s"\\\']*)?\'\nfor match in re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE):\n    pdf_urls.add(match)\nprint(f"    Total after regex fallback: {len(pdf_urls)} candidates.")\n\n# 4) Filter for likely University of Leicester domains\nprint("[STEP] Filtering for Leicester-related domains...")\ndomains = (\'le.ac.uk\', \'lra.le.ac.uk\', \'core.ac.uk\', \'hdl.handle.net\')\nleicester_links = [u for u in pdf_urls if any(d in u.lower() for d in domains)]\nif leicester_links:\n    print(f"    {len(leicester_links)} candidate(s) match Leicester domains:")\n    for u in leicester_links:\n        print(f"      - {u}")\nelse:\n    print("    No Leicester-specific candidates found; reporting all.")\n\n# --- Save all candidates for manual inspection ---\nwith open(out_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for url in sorted(pdf_urls):\n        f.write(url + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"\\n[SAVE] All PDF URL candidates written to: {out_path}")\n\nprint("[COMPLETE] Extraction of PDF link candidates is done. Inspect the output file and domain-filtered list.")',

Please run the search script first.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nif not os.path.isfile(html_file):\n    print(f"ERROR: Bing search HTML not found at {html_file}. Please generate it first.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Reading Bing HTML from: {html_file}\\n")\nwith open(html_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\n\n# --- Find all occurrences of \'.pdf\' (case-insensitive) ---\npdf_indices = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(r"\\.pdf", html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)]\ncount = len(pdf_indices)\nprint(f"[SCAN] Found {count} occurrences of \'.pdf\' in the HTML\\n")\n\n# --- Extract context snippets around each occurrence ---\ncontext_radius = 200  # characters before and after\nmax_snippets = 20      # limit number of snippets to save\nsnippets = []\nfor idx in pdf_indices[:max_snippets]:\n    start = max(idx - context_radius, 0)\n    end = min(idx + context_radius, len(html))\n    snippet = html[start:end]\n    # normalize whitespace for readability\n    snippet = snippet.replace(\'\\n\', \' \').replace(\'\\r\', \'\')\n    snippets.append(snippet)\n\n# --- Save snippets to file ---\nwith open(snippets_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as out:\n    for snip in snippets:\n        out.write(snip + \'\\n\' + \'-\'*60 + \'\\n\')\n\nprint(f"[SAVE] Wrote {len(snippets)} context snippets to: {snippets_file}\\n")\n\n# --- Print first few snippets for quick inspection ---\nprint("[PREVIEW] First 5 PDF-context snippets:\\n")\nfor i, snip in enumerate(snippets[:5], 1):\n    print(f"--- Snippet {i} ---\\n{snip}\\n")',
    "description": 'This script locates and surfaces every instance of “.pdf” in the saved Bing search HTML so we can discover how PDF URLs are actually embedded. It:\n1. Verifies the existence of `workspace/bing_search.html`.\n2. Loads the raw HTML and scans for the literal string “.pdf” (case-insensitive).\n3. Extracts up to the first 20 context snippets (200 characters on each side) around each occurrence.\n4. Saves these snippets to `workspace/pdf_snippets_v2.txt` for manual inspection.\n5. \'workspace\'\nbing_html_path = os.path.join(workspace, \'bing_search.html\')\nout_pdf_candidates = os.path.join(workspace, \'found_pdf_urls.txt\')\n\n# --- Ensure workspace exists ---\nif not ---\nquery = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon’s Diet? filetype:pdf site:le.ac.uk"\nbing_url = \'https://www.bing.com/search\'\nparams = {\'q\': query}\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64; rv:104.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/104.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n}\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Sending Bing search request with query:\\n      {query}\\n")\nresponse = requests.get(bing_url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=30)\nprint(f"[INFO] Bing response status: {response.status_code}")\n\nif response.status_code != 200:\n    print(f"ERROR: Bing search failed with status {response.status_code}\\nResponse body:\\n{response.text[:500]}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Save search HTML\nwith open(bing_html_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write(response.text)\nprint(f"[SAVE] Search page saved to: {bing_html_path}\\n")\n\n# --- Step 2: Load HTML and extract PDF candidates ---\nprint(f"[INFO] Parsing HTML for PDF URLs...")\nwith open(bing_html_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\npdf_urls = set()\n\n# 2a) Direct <a href> that endswith .pdf or contains .pdf?\nprint("[STEP] Scanning <a> tags for literal .pdf links...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in href.lower():\n        pdf_urls.add(href)\nprint(f"    Found {len(pdf_urls)} literal PDF href(s)")\n\n# 2b) Handle Bing redirect links (/url?q=...)\nprint("[STEP] Parsing Bing redirect links (/url?q=...pdf)...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.startswith(\'/url?\') or \'bing.com/url?\' in href:\n        parsed = urlparse(href)\n        qs = parse_qs(parsed.query)\n        for key in (\'q\', \'u\', \'url\'):\n            if key in qs:\n                real_url = unquote(qs[key][0])\n                if real_url.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in real_url.lower():\n                    pdf_urls.add(real_url)\n                break\nprint(f"    Total after redirect parsing: {len(pdf_urls)} re.findall(regex, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE):\n    pdf_urls.add(match)\nprint(f"    Total after regex fallback: {len(pdf_urls)} candidate(s)")\n\n# 2d) Filter for Leicester domains\nprint("[STEP] Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Save the raw HTML for inspection\nwith open(bing_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write(response.text)\nprint(f"[SAVE] Search results saved to: {bing_html}\\n")\n\n# --- Step 2: Parse the HTML and extract PDF URLs ---\nprint("[INFO] Parsing saved HTML to extract .pdf URLs...")\nwith open(bing_html, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\npdf_urls = set()\n\n# 2a) Direct <a> tags ending with .pdf or containing .pdf?\nprint("[STEP] Scanning <a> tags for literal .pdf links...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    low = href.lower()\n    if low.endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in low:\n        pdf_urls.add(href)\nprint(f"    Found {len(pdf_urls)} direct .pdf href(s)")\n\n# 2b) Parse Bing redirect links (/url?q=...)\nprint("[STEP] Parsing Bing redirect links for .pdf URLs...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.startswith(\'/url?\') or \'bing.com/url?\' in href:\n        parsed = urlparse(href)\n        qs = parse_qs(parsed.query)\n        for key in (\'q\',\'u\',\'url\'):\n            if key in qs:\n                real = unquote(qs[key][0])\n                lowr = real.lower()\n                if lowr.endswith(\'.pdf\') or \'.pdf?\' in lowr:\n                    pdf_urls.add(real)\n                break\nprint(f"    Total after redirect parsing: {len(pdf_urls)} candidate(s)")\n\n# 2c) Regex fallback on raw HTML\nprint("[STEP] Running regex fallback for html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\nfor m in matches:\n    pdf_urls.add(m)\nprint(f"    Total after regex fallback: {len(pdf_urls)} candidate(s)")\n\n# 2d) Filter for Leicester-related domains\nprint("[STEP] Filtering for Leicester domains (le.ac.uk, lra.le.ac.uk, core.ac.uk, hdl.handle.net)...")\ndomains = (\'le.ac.uk\',\'lra.le.ac.uk\',\'core.ac.uk\',\'hdl.handle.net\')\nle_urls = [u for u in pdf_urls encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for u in sorted(pdf_urls):\n        f.write(u + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"\\n[SAVE] All PDF URL candidates written to: {candidates_out}")\nprint("[COMPLETE] Extraction phase     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Paths ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nbing_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'bing_search.html\')\ninspection_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'search_results_inspection.txt\')\n\n# --- Ensure input exists ---\nif not os.path.isfile(bing_html):\n    print(f"ERROR: Cannot find Bing HTML at {bing_html}. Please run the search extraction first.")\n    exit(1)\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Inspecting Bing search HTML: {bing_html}\\n")\nwith open(bing_html, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 1) Extract main result anchors (li.b_algo > h2 > a)\nanchors = soup.select(\'li.b_algo h2 a\')\nprint(f"[INSPECT] Found {len(anchors)} main result links (li.b_algo h2 a). Listing top 10:\\n")\n\nwith open(inspection_out, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as out:\n    out.write(f"Main result links (total: {len(anchors)})\\n")\n    out.write("="*60 + "\\n")\n    for i, a in enumerate(anchors[:10], 1):\n        title = a.get_text(strip=True)\n        href = a.get(\'href\')\n        line = f"{i}. Title: {title}\\n   URL:  {href}\\n"\n        print(line)\n        out.write(line + "\\n")\n\n# 2) Scan for any <a> elements whose text or href contains \'.pdf\'\npdf_links = []\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    txt = a.get_text()\n    if \'.pdf\' in href.lower() or \'.pdf\' in txt.lower():\n        pdf_links.append((txt.strip(), href))\n\nprint(f"[INSPECT] Found {len(pdf_links)} <a> tags with \'.pdf\' in text or href. Listing top 10:\\n")\nout.write(f"\\nPDF-like <a> tags (total: {len(pdf_links)})\\n")\nout.write("="*60 + "\\n")\nfor i, (txt, href) in enumerate(pdf_links[:10], 1):\n    line = f"{i}. Text: {txt or \'[no text]\'}\\n   Href: {href}\\n"\n    print(line)\n    out.write(line + "\\n")\n\n# 3) Summarize\nsummary = (\n    f"\\n=== SUMMARY ===\\n"\n    f"Total main result anchors (li.b_algo h2 a): {len(anchors)}\\n"\n    f"Total PDF-like <a> tags: {len(pdf_links)}\\n"\n)\nprint(summary)\nout.write(summary)\n\nprint(f"[SAVE] Inspection details written to: {inspection_out}")\nprint("[COMPLETE] Please open the inspection file to understand the HTML structure and adjust your extraction logic accordingly.")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nimport re\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nfrom urllib.parse import urlparse, parse_qs, unquote\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nbing_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'bing_search.html\')\ncandidates_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'found_pdf_urls.txt\')\n\n# --- Ensure workspace exists ---\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    print(f"[INFO] Creating workspace directory: {workspace}")\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# --- Step 1: Perform a broader Bing search for any PDF of the paper ---\nquery = "filetype:pdf \\"Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon’s Diet?\\""\nbing_url = \'https://www.bing.com/search\'\nparams = {\'q\': query, \'count\': \'50\'}  # fetch more results\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64; rv:104.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/104.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n}\nprint(f"[INFO] Sending Bing search request with query:\\n      {query}\\n")\nresponse = requests.get(bing_url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=30)\nprint(f"[INFO] Bing returned status: {response.status_code}")\nif response.status_code != 200:\n    print(f"ERROR: Bing search failed with status {response.status_code}. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Save raw HTML for inspection\nwith open(bing_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write(response.text)\nprint(f"[SAVE] Bing search HTML → {bing_html}\\n")\n\n# --- Step 2: Parse HTML and extract candidate PDF URLs ---\nprint("[INFO] Parsing HTML and extracting PDF URLs...")\nwith open(bing_html, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    html = f.read()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n\npdf_urls = set()\n\n# 2a) Extract main result anchors (li.b_algo h2 a)\nanchors = soup.select(\'li.b_algo h2 a\')\nprint(f"[STEP] Found {len(anchors)} main result anchors. Scanning for .pdf links...")\nfor a in anchors:\n    href = a.get(\'href\') or \'\'\n    if \'.pdf\' in href.lower():\n        pdf_urls.add(href)\n        print(f"    [FOUND] PDF in result anchor: {href}")\n\n# 2b) Decode Bing redirect links (/url?q=...)\nprint(f"[STEP] Parsing Bing redirect links for PDFs...")\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    if href.startswith(\'/url?\') or \'bing.com/url?\' in href:\n        parsed = urlparse(href)\n        qs = parse_qs(parsed.query)\n        for key in (\'q\',\'u\',\'url\'):\n            if key in qs:\n                real = unquote(qs[key][0])\n                if \'.pdf\' in real.lower():\n                    pdf_urls.add(real)\n                    print(f"    [FOUND] PDF in redirect URL: {real}")\n                break\n\n# 2c) Regex fallback over raw HTML\nprint("[STEP] Running regex fallback for http(s)://...pdf patterns...")\npattern = r\'\'\'https?://[^\\s"\']+?\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s"\']*)?\'\'\'\nmatches = re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE)\nfor m in matches:\n    pdf_urls.add(m)\nprint(f"    [INFO] Total after regex fallback: {len(pdf_urls)} candidates")\n\n# 2d) Filter for University of Leicester domains\nprint("[STEP] Filtering for University of Leicester domains...")\nleicester_domains = (\'le.ac.uk\',\'lra.le.ac.uk\')\nle_urls = [u for u in pdf_urls if any(d in u.lower() for d in leicester_domains)]\nif le_urls:\n    print(f"    [SUCCESS] Found {len(le_urls)} Leicester PDF URL(s):")\n    for u in le_urls:\n        print(f"      - {u}")\nelse:\n    print("    [WARN] No Leicester-specific PDFs found. Listing all candidates:")\n    for u in sorted(pdf_urls):\n        print(f"      - {u}")\n\n# Save all candidates\nwith open(candidates_out, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for u in sorted(pdf_urls):\n        f.write(u + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"\\n[SAVE] All PDF candidates written to: {candidates_out}")\nprint("[COMPLETE] Extraction phase finished. Inspect the file to choose the correct PDF link.")\n',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import quote, urljoin\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Base for Leicester Research Archive (DSpace)\nbase_url = \'https://lra.le.ac.uk\'\n# Paper title (using ASCII apostrophe)\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n# Build search URL (DSpace simple-search)\nencoded = quote(f\'"{title}"\')\nsearch_url = f\'{base_url}/simple-search?query={encoded}\'\n\n# Paths for saving intermediate files\nsearch_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'lra_search.html\')\ncandidates_txt = os.path.join(workspace, \'lra_pdf_urls.txt\')\npdf_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Searching DSpace for paper: {title}")\nprint(f"[INFO] GET {search_url}")\nresp = requests.get(search_url, timeout=30)\nprint(f"[INFO] Search page response: {resp.status_code}")\nif resp.status_code != 200:\n    print("ERROR: Failed to fetch search page.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Save search HTML for inspection\nwith open(search_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write(resp.text)\nprint(f"[SAVE] Search HTML → {search_html}")\n\n# Parse HTML and extract PDF links\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\npdf_links = set()\n\n# Strategy: find anchors that either end in .pdf or whose text mentions PDF\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    txt = a.get_text(strip=True).lower()\n    # detect direct PDF files or DSpace bitstream links\n    if href.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or (\'.pdf\' in href.lower() and \'bitstream\' in href.lower()):\n        pdf_links.add(href)\n    # also check link text for \'pdf\'\n    elif \'pdf\' in txt:\n        pdf_links.add(href)\n\n# Normalize and filter full URLs\nfull_links = []\nfor link in pdf_links:\n    if link.startswith(\'http\'):\n        full = link\n    else:\n        full = urljoin(base_url, link)\n    full_links.append(full)\n\n# Write candidates to file\nwith open(candidates_txt, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for u in full_links:\n        f.write(u + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"[SAVE] Candidate PDF URLs → {candidates_txt}")\n\n# If found, download the first candidate\nif full_links:\n    first = full_links[0]\n    print(f"[INFO] Downloading paper PDF from: {first}")\n    pdf_resp = requests.get(first, timeout=60)\n    print(f"[INFO] PDF download status: {pdf_resp.status_code}")\n    if pdf_resp.status_code == 200 and len(pdf_resp.content) > 10000:\n        with open(pdf_out, \'wb\') as f:\n            f.write(pdf_resp.content)\n        size = os.path.getsize(pdf_out)\n        print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF → {pdf_out} ({size} bytes)")\n    else:\n        print("ERROR: Download failed or file too small. Content-Type/size may be incorrect.")\n        print(f"Content length: {len(pdf_resp.content)} bytes")\nelse:\n    print("WARN: No PDF links found on the repository search page.")\n    print("Please inspect \'lra_search.html\' and adjust search or selectors accordingly.")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import quote, urljoin\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Suppress SSL warnings and bypass verification ---\nimport requests.packages.urllib3\nrequests.packages.urllib3.disable_warnings()\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Base for Leicester Research Archive (DSpace)\nbase_url = \'https://lra.le.ac.uk\'\n# Paper title (using ASCII apostrophe)\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n# Build search URL (DSpace simple-search)\nencoded = quote(f\'"{title}"\')\nsearch_url = f\'{base_url}/simple-search?query={encoded}\'\n\n# Paths for saving intermediate files\nsearch_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'lra_search.html\')\ncandidates_txt = os.path.join(workspace, \'lra_pdf_urls.txt\')\npdf_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\nprint(f"[INFO] Searching DSpace for paper: {title}")\nprint(f"[INFO] GET {search_url} (verify=False)")\ntry:\n    resp = requests.get(search_url, verify=False, timeout=30)\n    print(f"[INFO] Search page response status: {resp.status_code}")\nexcept requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:\n    print(f"ERROR: Failed to fetch search page due to: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nif resp.status_code != 200:\n    print(f"ERROR: Unexpected status code {resp.status_code} for search page.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Save search HTML for inspection\nwith open(search_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write(resp.text)\nprint(f"[SAVE] Search HTML → {search_html}")\n\n# Parse HTML and extract PDF links\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\npdf_links = set()\n\n# Strategy: find anchors that either end in .pdf or whose text mentions PDF or contain \'bitstream\'\nfor a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n    href = a[\'href\']\n    txt = a.get_text(strip=True).lower()\n    # detect direct PDF files or DSpace bitstream links\n    if href.lower().endswith(\'.pdf\') or (\'bitstream\' in href.lower() and \'.pdf\' in href.lower()):\n        pdf_links.add(href)\n    # also check link text for \'pdf\'\n    elif \'pdf\' in txt:\n        pdf_links.add(href)\n\n# Normalize and filter full URLs\nfull_links = []\nfor link in pdf_links:\n    if link.startswith(\'http\'):\n        full = link\n    else:\n        full = urljoin(base_url, link)\n    full_links.append(full)\n\n# Write candidates to file\nwith open(candidates_txt, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for u in full_links:\n        f.write(u + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"[SAVE] Candidate PDF URLs → {candidates_txt}")\n\n# If found, download the first candidate\nif full_links:\n    first = full_links[0]\n    print(f"[INFO] Attempting to download paper PDF from: {first} (verify=False)")\n    try:\n        pdf_resp = requests.get(first, verify=False, timeout=60)\n        print(f"[INFO] PDF download status: {pdf_resp.status_code}")\n    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:\n        print(f"ERROR: PDF download failed due to: {e}")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    if pdf_resp.status_code == 200 and len(pdf_resp.content) > 10000:\n        with open(pdf_out, \'wb\') as f:\n            f.write(pdf_resp.content)\n        size = os.path.getsize(pdf_out)\n        print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF → {pdf_out} ({size} bytes)")\n    else:\n        print("ERROR: Download failed or file too small. Check link and try again.")\n        print(f"Content length: {len(pdf_resp.content)} bytes")\nelse:\n    print("WARN: No PDF links found on the repository search page.")\n    print("Please inspect \'lra_search.html\' and adjust the selection logic accordingly.")',

Check the link and try again.")\n        print(f"Content length: {len(pdf_resp.content)} bytes")\nelse:\n    print("WARN: No PDF links found on search page. Please inspect \'lra_search.html\' for correct link patterns.")\n    print("Adjust link-selection logic or try a different repository endpoint.")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nimport re\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# The paper title\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n# DuckDuckGo HTML search endpoint\nddg_url = \'https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/\'\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\'\n}\n\n# Queries to try: first restrict to Leicester domains, then broad\nqueries = [\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:lra.le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}"\'\n]\n\n# Paths\nddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_search.html\')\npdf_list = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_pdf_urls.txt\')\npdf_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\nall_candidates = []\n\n# Perform searches\nfor q in queries:\n    print(f"[INFO] DuckDuckGo search query: {q}")\n    resp = requests.post(ddg_url, data={\'q\': q}, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    print(f"[INFO] Response status: {resp.status_code}")\n    if resp.status_code != 200:\n        print(f"[WARN] Non-200 status for query \'{q}\', skipping.")\n        continue\n\n    # Save the first search HTML for inspection\n    if not os.path.exists(ddg_html):\n        with open(ddg_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(resp.text)\n        print(f"[SAVE] DuckDuckGo HTML → {ddg_html}")\n\n    html = resp.text\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n    candidates = set()\n\n    # 1) Extract anchors with href containing .pdf\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        if \'.pdf\' in href.lower():\n            candidates.add(href)\n            print(f"    [FOUND] PDF link in anchor: {href}")\n\n    # 2) Regex fallback on raw HTML\n    pattern = r\'https?://[^\\s"\']+?\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s"\']*)?\'\n    for match in re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE):\n        if match not in candidates:\n            candidates.add(match)\n            print(f"    [FOUND] PDF via regex: {match}")\n\n    # Normalize and collect full URLs\n    for link in candidates:\n        # DuckDuckGo sometimes wraps real URLs in \'/l/?kh=-1&uddg=\'\n        if \'uddg=\' in link:\n            # Extract after uddg=\n            real = re.search(r\'uddg=(.+)\', link)\n            if real:\n                url = requests.utils.unquote(real.group(1))\n            else:\n                url = link\n        else:\n            url = link\n        all_candidates.append(url)\n\n    if all_candidates:\n        print(f"[INFO] Found {len(all_candidates)} PDF candidate(s). Stopping further queries.")\n        break\n    else:\n        print(f"[INFO] No PDF links found for query \'{q}\'. Trying next query.\\n")\n\n# Save all candidates\nif all_candidates:\n    unique = []\n    for u in all_candidates:\n        if u not in unique:\n            unique.append(u)\n    with open(pdf_list, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        for u in unique:\n            f.write(u + \'\\n\')\n    print(f"[SAVE] Candidate PDF URLs → {pdf_list}")\nelse:\n    print("[ERROR] No PDF candidates found after all queries.")\n    print(f"Please inspect \'{ddg_html}\' and adjust the query or parsing logic.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Download the first candidate\nfirst = unique[0]\nprint(f"[INFO] Downloading PDF from: {first}")\ntry:\n    dl = requests.get(first, headers=headers, timeout=60)\n    print(f"[INFO] Download status: {dl.status_code}")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to download PDF: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nif dl.status_code == 200 and len(dl.content) > 10_000:\n    with open(pdf_out, \'wb\') as f:\n        f.write(dl.content)\n    size = os.path.getsize(pdf_out)\n    print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF → {pdf_out} ({size} bytes)")\nelse:\n    print("[ERROR] Download failed or file too small (<10 KB).")\n    print(f"Content length: {len(dl.content)} bytes")\n    print(f"Inspect \'{pdf_list}\', pick another link, and try manually.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n',

{
    "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# The exact paper title to search for\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n# DuckDuckGo HTML search endpoint\nddg_url = \'https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/\'\n# Browser-like headers to avoid blocking\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\'\n}\n\n# Three successive queries: restrict to Leicester archive, then broad site, then global PDF search\nqueries = [\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:lra.le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}"\'\n]\n\n# Paths for saving outputs\nddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_search.html\')\npdf_list = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_pdf_urls.txt\')\npdf_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\nall_candidates = []\n\n# Perform each DuckDuckGo query until we find PDF links\nfor q in queries:\n    print(f"[INFO] DuckDuckGo search query: {q}")\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(ddg_url, data={\'q\': q}, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"[WARN] Request error for query \'{q}\': {e}")\n        continue\n\n    print(f"[INFO] Response status: {resp.status_code}")\n    if resp.status_code != 200:\n        print(f"[WARN] Non-200 status for query \'{q}\', skipping.")\n        continue\n\n    # Save the first successful HTML page for inspection\n    if not os.path.exists(ddg_html):\n        with open(ddg_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(resp.text)\n        print(f"[SAVE] DuckDuckGo HTML → {ddg_html}")\n\n    html = resp.text\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n    candidates = set()\n\n    # 1) Extract direct <a> hrefs containing \'.pdf\'\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        if \'.pdf\' in href.lower():\n            candidates.add(href)\n            print(f"    [FOUND] PDF link in anchor: {href}")\n\n    # 2) Regex fallback to catch raw PDF URLs\n    pattern = r"""https?://[^\\s"\']+?\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\s"\']*)?"""\n    for match in re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE):\n        candidates.add(match)\n        print(f"    [FOUND] PDF via regex: {match}")\n\n    # Decode any DuckDuckGo redirect wrappers (uddg=)\n    for link in candidates:\n        if \'uddg=\' in link:\n            real_match = re.search(r\'uddg=([^&]+)\', link)\n            url = requests.utils.unquote(real_match.group(1)) if real_match else link\n        else:\n            url = link\n        all_candidates.append(url)\n\n    if all_candidates:\n        print(f"[INFO] Found {len(all_candidates)} PDF candidate(s). Stopping.")\n        break\n    else:\n        print(f"[INFO] No PDF links for query \'{q}\'.     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# --- Configuration ---\nworkspace = \'workspace\'\nif not os.path.isdir(workspace):\n    os.makedirs(workspace, exist_ok=True)\n\n# The exact paper title to search for\ntitle = "Can Hiccup Supply Enough Fish to Maintain a Dragon\'s Diet?"\n# DuckDuckGo HTML search endpoint\nddg_url = \'https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/\'\n# Browser-like headers to avoid being blocked by simple filters\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\'\n}\n\n# Three successive queries: restrict to Leicester archive, then broader, then global PDF search\nqueries = [\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:lra.le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}" site:le.ac.uk\',\n    f\'filetype:pdf "{title}"\'\n]\n\n# Paths for outputs\nddg_html = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_search.html\')\npdf_list = os.path.join(workspace, \'ddg_pdf_urls.txt\')\npdf_out = os.path.join(workspace, \'dragon_diet_fish_bag.pdf\')\n\nall_candidates = []\n\n# Iterate through search queries until we find PDF links\nfor q in queries:\n    print(f"[INFO] DuckDuckGo search query: {q}")\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(ddg_url, data={\'q\': q}, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"[WARN] Request error for query \'{q}\': {e}")\n        continue\n\n    status = resp.status_code\n    print(f"[INFO] Response status: {status}")\n    # Accept any 2xx status as success\n    if status < 200 or status >= 300:\n        print(f"[WARN] Non-2xx status for query \'{q}\', skipping.\\n")\n        continue\n\n    # Save the first successful HTML page for manual inspection\n    if not os.path.exists(ddg_html):\n        with open(ddg_html, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(resp.text)\n        print(f"[SAVE] DuckDuckGo HTML → {ddg_html}")\n\n    html = resp.text\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, \'html.parser\')\n    candidates = set()\n\n    # 1) Extract <a> tags with href containing \'.pdf\'\n    for a in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = a[\'href\']\n        if \'.pdf\' in href.lower():\n            candidates.add(href)\n            print(f"    [FOUND] PDF link in anchor: {href}")\n\n    # 2) Regex fallback to catch raw PDF URLs\n    # Properly quoted regex string to avoid unmatched bracket errors\n    pattern = r"https?://[^\\s\\"\']+?\\.pdf(?:\\?[^\\"\'\\s]*)?"\n    for match in re.findall(pattern, html, flags=re.IGNORECASE):\n        candidates.add(match)\n        print(f"    [FOUND] PDF via regex: {match}")\n\n    # Decode any DuckDuckGo redirect wrappers (uddg=)\n    for link in candidates:\n        if \'uddg=\' in link:\n            m = re.search(r\'uddg=([^&]+)\', link)\n            url = requests.utils.unquote(m.group(1)) if m else link\n        else:\n            url = link\n        all_candidates.append(url)\n\n    if all_candidates:\n        print(f"[INFO] Found {len(all_candidates)} PDF candidate(s). Stopping further queries.")\n        break\n    else:\n        print(f"[INFO] No PDF links for query \'{q}\'. Trying next.\\n")\n\n# If still no candidates, exit with error\nif not all_candidates:\n    print("[ERROR] No PDF candidates found after all queries.")\n    print(f"Inspect \'{ddg_html}\' and refine search or parsing logic.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# Deduplicate and save candidate list\nunique = []\nfor u in all_candidates:\n    if u not in unique:\n        unique.append(u)\nwith open(pdf_list, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    for u in unique:\n        f.write(u + \'\\n\')\nprint(f"[SAVE] Candidate PDF URLs → {pdf_list}")\n\n# Function to download a PDF\ndef download_pdf(url, out_path):\n    print(f"[INFO] Downloading PDF from: {url}")\n    try:\n        dl = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=60)\n        print(f"[INFO] Download status: {dl.status_code}")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"[ERROR] Download failed: {e}")\n        return False\n    if dl.status_code == 200 and len(dl.content) > 10_000:\n        with open(out_path, \'wb\') as f:\n            f.write(dl.content)\n        size = os.path.getsize(out_path)\n        print(f"[SUCCESS] Saved PDF → {out_path} ({size} bytes)")\n        return True\n    else:\n        print(f"[ERROR] Download returned status {dl.status_code} or file too small ({len(dl.content)} bytes)")\n        return False\n\n# Attempt download of the first candidate\nfirst_url = unique[0]\nif not download_pdf(first_url, pdf_out):\n    print(f"[ERROR] Could not download from first URL. Try another link from {pdf_list}.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n',
